		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:center;font-family:Symbol;color:#000000;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-size:10pt;">~ Second quarter consolidated net sales grew by 12 percent compared to prior year fiscal quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;font-size:10pt;">~</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;We continue to experience very high demand for our maintenance products due to renovation trends associated with the pandemic,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> or what we call </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">isolation renovation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; said Garry Ridge, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s chairman and chief executive officer. &#x201C;In addition, we are seeing </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">improved market conditions due to a reduction of COVID-19 lockdown measures in many markets, particularly in China, as well as increased sales through the ecommerce channel</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&#x201D;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">However, the pandemic has also caused some disruptions and constraints to our supply chain, primarily in the Americas, which impacted our ability to meet </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">end</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">user demand </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">we experienced in</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the United States </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">during</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the second quarter.&nbsp;&nbsp;Despite these supply chain challenges in the United States, we continue to experience very strong point-of-sale end</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">user demand for our maintenance products. We are working to address the supply chain challenges and there is a recovery plan underway</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which we expect will result in improved conditions in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">back half of the year.&#x201D;&nbsp; </font>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;We are off to a very strong start in the first half of fiscal 2021. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">K</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">eeping up with demand in a COVID environment has been a challenge</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> but we&#x2019;ve increased our revenue expectations and believe that net sales are likely to be in a range of between $445 million to $475 million for the full fiscal year.&nbsp;&nbsp;This upward revision is driven primarily by favorable changes in foreign currency exchange rates.&nbsp;&nbsp;Additionally, over the long-term, we are optimistic that many of the new end</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">users who have interacted with our products during the pandemic will become permanent users of our maintenance and homecare solutions,&#x201D; Ridge concluded.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:12pt;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font>
		</p>
		<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">

		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"></font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"></font>

		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">19</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to higher sales of maintenance products in both the EMEA direct and distributor markets, which increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">7 percent and 3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent, respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;Higher sales of maintenance products in the EMEA direct markets were primarily due to increased sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product driven by increased demand linked to renovation trends associated with the pandemic and increased sales through the ecommerce channel. Higher sales of maintenance products in the EMEA distributor markets were primarily attributable to improved economic conditions as a result of reductions in COVID-19 related movement restrictions.&nbsp;&nbsp;Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a favorable impact on sales for the EMEA segment from period to period. On a constant currency basis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> EMEA sales for the first quarter would have increased by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">15</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent compared to the prior </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">fiscal year quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;background-color:#FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific increased 39 percent in the second quarter due primarily to higher sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in China which increased 251 percent compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior year fiscal quarter.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> Higher sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product in China were primarily due to improved market conditions </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the reduction of COVID-19 lockdown measures compared to the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year when the pandemic was in its earliest stages.&nbsp;&nbsp;Also contributing to higher sales in Asia-Pacific were higher sales in Australia which increased 39 percent compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior year fiscal quarter.&nbsp;&nbsp;This increase</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> was driven by higher demand for maintenance products linked to renovation trends and increased demand for cleaning products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">impacts of the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">pandemic.&nbsp;&nbsp;Partially offsetting these increases were lower sales in the Asia-Pacific distributor markets which declined 4 percent compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;background-color: #FFFFFF;">prior year fiscal quarter.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> The lower sales of maintenance products in the Asia distributor markets were attributed to the shift in the timing of customer orders a</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">s well as</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> delays in the shipment of certain orders linked to shipping container shortages</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in the region</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, many of the Company&#x2019;s marketing distributors are continuing to adjust to more normalized inventory levels. Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a favorable impact on sales for the Asia-Pacific segment. On a constant currency basis, Asia-Pacific would have increased by 32 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0.1pt 36pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>

		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company markets a wide range of maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;, Lava&#xAE; and Solvol&#xAE;.&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x2003;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $408.5 million in fiscal year 2020 and its products are currently available in more than 176 countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
